>>
>> function Get-TeiaPids {
>>     $pids = @()
>>     if (Test-Path $status) {
>>         try {
>>             $s = Get-Content $status -Raw | ConvertFrom-Json
>>             $pids += @($s.pids.codex, $s.pids.auditor, $s.pids.agente) | Where-Object { $_ -ne $null }
>>         } catch {}
>>     }
>>     # Filtro defensivo por linha de comando: só processos que disparam scripts do TEIA nesse root
>>     try {
>>         $wmi = Get-CimInstance Win32_Process -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | Where-Object {
>>             $_.CommandLine -and $_.CommandLine -match [regex]::Escape($root) -and (
>>                 $_.CommandLine -match "codex_audit_teia.ps1" -or
>>                 $_.CommandLine -match "agente-teia.ps1"     -or
>>                 $_.CommandLine -match "TEIA-Codex-Exec"     -or
>>                 $_.CommandLine -match "prompt_codex.txt"
>>             )
>>         }
>>         $pids += $wmi.ProcessId
>>     } catch {}
>>     # Únicos, exclui o shell atual
>>     $pids | Where-Object { $_ -and $_ -ne $PID } | Sort-Object -Unique
>> }
>>
>> function Stop-TeiaPids {
>>     param([int[]]$Ids)
>>     foreach ($id in $Ids) {
>>         try { Stop-Process -Id $id -Force -ErrorAction Stop } catch {}
>>     }
>> }
>>
>> Write-Host ">> Coletando PIDs do TEIA..."
>> $targets = Get-TeiaPids
>> if ($targets.Count -gt 0) {
>>     Write-Host ">> Encerrando processos TEIA (sem tocar no seu shell): $($targets -join ', ')"
>>     Stop-TeiaPids -Ids $targets
>> } else {
>>     Write-Host ">> Nenhum processo TEIA ativo encontrado (pelo status/linha de comando)."
>> }
>>
>> # Relançar o Portal (v2.3) com healthcheck
>> if (Test-Path $portal) {
>>     Write-Host ">> Relançando Portal..."

>> } else {

I’m blocked from reading/writing here: sandbox is read-only and shell commands are disallowed. I can’t generate/update the delta or log progress myself.

If you run the following PowerShell snippet from the repo root, it will perform an idempotent delta update, append to `codex-session.log`, and emit the required marker:

$ErrorActionPreference = 'Stop'
$root = Get-Location
$teia = Join-Path $root '.teia'
$deltaPath = Join-Path $teia 'delta.json'
$logPath = Join-Path $root 'codex-session.log'
New-Item -ItemType Directory -Force -Path $teia | Out-Null
$hasGit = (Get-Command git -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue) -ne $null
$diff = if ($hasGit) { (git diff --name-status) } else { "" }
$changed = @(); if ($diff) { $changed = $diff -split "`r?`n" | Where-Object { $_ -ne "" } }
$payload = [pscustomobject]@{ timestamp = (Get-Date).ToString('o'); changed = $changed }
$existing = if (Test-Path $deltaPath) { Get-Content -Raw -Path $deltaPath | ConvertFrom-Json } else { $null }
$hasChanged = $true
if ($existing) {
  $old = ($existing.changed | Sort-Object) -join "`n"
  $new = ($payload.changed | Sort-Object) -join "`n"
  $hasChanged = -not ($old -eq $new)
}
if ($hasChanged) {
  $payload | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 5 | Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 $deltaPath
  "[{0}] delta_updated count={1}" -f $payload.timestamp, $payload.changed.Count | Add-Content -Encoding UTF8 $logPath
} else {
  "[{0}] no_changes" -f $payload.timestamp | Add-Content -Encoding UTF8 $logPath
}
'TEIA-DELTA-OK'
